Actor Cultist		
{
	Health 40
	Radius 20 
	Height 56 
	Speed 2.88
	Scale 0.53
	MinMissileChance 230
	PainChance 192
	+FLOORCLIP 
	+NOINFIGHTING
	+NOBLOODDECALS
	Monster
	PainChance "CalebFire", 0
	PainChance "MightyBoot", 255
	PainChance "MarathonStun", 255
	Species "Enemies"
	SeeSound "cultistsee"
	PainSound "cultistpain"
	DeathSound "cultistdie"
	ActiveSound "cultistact"
	DropItem "RandomCultistDrop"
	BloodType "NashGore_Blood_Monolith"	
	Obituary "%o was shot by a cultist."
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	States
	{ 
	Spawn:
		YCUF A 0
		YCUF A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
		YCUF A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
		YCUF A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
	Spawn2:	
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,3)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(184,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("CultistIsCrawling",1)
		TNT1 AA 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("CultistTaunt_Enemy",1,"Curse")	
	SpawnLoop:		
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("CultistIsCrawling",1,"SpawnCrawl")	
		YCUF A 5 A_Look
		Loop	
	SpawnCrawl:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(FRIGHTENED,0)	
	SpawnCrawlLoop:
		YCUB N 5 A_Look
		Loop		
	Curse:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("CultistGotYou",CHAN_VOICE,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("CultistTaunt_Enemy",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("CultistIsCrawling",1)		
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(FRIGHTENED,0)		
	RoamLoop:	
		YCUL A 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look
		YCUL A 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL A 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL A 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look

		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL B 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL B 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL B 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL C 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL C 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL C 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL C 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL D 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL D 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL D 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look
		YCUL D 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL E 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL E 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL E 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL E 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL F 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL F 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL F 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUL F 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(5,"SpawnLoop")
		Loop
	BackToNormal:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(FRIGHTENED,0)		
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("CultistIsCrawling",1)		
	See: 
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("CultistTaunt_Enemy",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("CultistIsCrawling",1,"Crawling")				
	SeeLoop:	
		YCUL A 1 A_Chase("", "Missile",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUL A 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUL A 1 A_Chase 
		YCUL A 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUL B 1 A_Chase 
		YCUL B 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUL B 1 A_Chase("", "Missile",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE) 
		YCUL B 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUL C 1 A_Chase 
		YCUL C 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUL C 1 A_Chase 
		YCUL C 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUL D 1 A_Chase("", "Missile",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE) 
		YCUL D 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUL D 1 A_Chase 
		YCUL D 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUL E 1 A_Chase 
		YCUL E 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUL E 1 A_Chase("", "Missile",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE) 
		YCUL E 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUL F 1 A_Chase
		YCUL F 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUL F 1 A_Chase 
		YCUL F 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		Loop
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(220,"ASD")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(450,"TNTT")
	ASD:
		YCUF A 1 A_FaceTarget	
		TNT1 A 0 A_playsound("cultist/Fire")
		YCUF B 6 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(5.8,4.45,3,4,"ZBBulletPuff_2", 0, CBAF_NORANDOM)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(20,"Retreat")
		YCUF A 8 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(70,1)		
		YCUL A 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUL A 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_playsound("cultist/Fire")
		YCUF B 6 Bright A_CustomBulletAttack(5.8,4.45,3,4,"ZBBulletPuff_2",0, CBAF_NORANDOM)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(100,"Retreat")

		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(70,2)
		YCUL A 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUL A 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUL A 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUL A 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)

	    YCUF A 8 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See

		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(100,"See","ASD")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(15,"TNTT2")

		YCUL [ 4 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("Cultists/Toss",CHAN_AUTO)		
		YCUL ^ 4 A_CustomMissile("CultistTNT",30,0,0,CMF_OFFSETPITCH)
		YCUB A 4
		Goto See
	TNTT2:	
		YCUL XYZ 4 A_FaceTarget
		YCUL [ 4 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("TNT/Throw",CHAN_AUTO)		
		YCUL ^ 4 A_CustomMissile("PlCultistTNT_2",30,0,0,CMF_OFFSETPITCH)
		YCUB A 4
		Goto See

		YCUL G 30 A_Pain
		YCUL G 70
		Goto See

		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)

		TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
		YCUL G 16 A_Pain

		TNT1 A 0 A_Stop
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("NothingSpeed")

		YCUB L 1 A_Chase("", ""/*,CHF_NODIRECTIONTURN*/)
		YCUB L 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE/*|CHF_NODIRECTIONTURN*/)
		YCUB L 1 A_Chase("", ""/*,CHF_NODIRECTIONTURN*/)
		YCUB L 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE/*|CHF_NODIRECTIONTURN*/)
		YCUB M 1 A_Chase("", ""/*,CHF_NODIRECTIONTURN*/)
		YCUB M 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE/*|CHF_NODIRECTIONTURN*/)
		YCUB M 1 A_Chase("", ""/*,CHF_NODIRECTIONTURN*/)
		YCUB M 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE/*|CHF_NODIRECTIONTURN*/)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(FRIGHTENED,0)

		YCUB J 1 A_Chase("CrawlFire", ""/*,CHF_NODIRECTIONTURN*/)

		YCUB J 1 A_Chase("CrawlFire", ""/*,CHF_NODIRECTIONTURN*/) 
		YCUB J 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE/*|CHF_NODIRECTIONTURN*/)
		YCUB K 1 A_Chase("CrawlFire", ""/*,CHF_NODIRECTIONTURN*/)
		YCUB K 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE/*|CHF_NODIRECTIONTURN*/)
		YCUB K 1 A_Chase("CrawlFire", ""/*,CHF_NODIRECTIONTURN*/)

    Death:

		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("CultistIsCrawling",1)

		YCUL H 5 A_Scream
		YCUL I 5  
		YCUL J 5 
		YCUL K 5 A_Fall
		YCUL L 5
		TNT1 A 0 //A_SpawnItemEx("RandomCultistDrop",0,0,0,0,0,10,0,40)

		YCUL NON 5
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(68,"Dissolve1")

		YCUL O 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodCultistCorpse1", 0, 0, 0, velx, vely, velz, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_ABSOLUTEVELOCITY)

		YCUL ONO 5

			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}
}

actor Cultist_ShrinkEffect : Cultist
{
	-ISMONSTER
	-COUNTKILL
	-SHOOTABLE
	-SOLID
	+NOINTERACTION
	-NOGRAVITY
	+CLIENTSIDEONLY	
	Renderstyle Translucent
	Alpha 0.4
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			YCUL G 0
			YCUL G 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			YCUL G 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			Stop
	}
}

Actor Fanatic : Cultist
{
	Health 40
	DropItem "RandomFanaticDrop"
	Obituary "%o met a fanatic."
	SeeSound "Fanatic/See"
	PainSound "Fanatic/Pain"
	DeathSound "Fanatic/Die"
	ActiveSound "Fanatic/Act"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		YCU8 A 0
		YCU8 A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
		YCU8 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
		YCU8 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
	Spawn2:	 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,3)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(184,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("CultistIsCrawling",1)
		TNT1 AA 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("CultistTaunt_Enemy",1,"Curse")		
	SpawnLoop:	
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("CultistIsCrawling",1,"SpawnCrawl")	
		YCU8 A 5 A_Look
		Loop	
	SpawnCrawl:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(FRIGHTENED,0)	
	SpawnCrawlLoop:
		YCU9 N 5 A_Look
		Loop		
	Curse:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("Fanatic/GotYou",CHAN_VOICE,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("CultistTaunt_Enemy",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("CultistIsCrawling",1)		
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(FRIGHTENED,0)				
	RoamLoop:	
		YCUG A 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look
		YCUG A 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG A 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG A 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG B 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG B 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG B 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG B 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG C 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG C 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG C 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG C 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG D 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG D 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG D 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look
		YCUG D 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG E 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG E 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG E 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG E 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG F 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG F 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG F 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUG F 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(5,"SpawnLoop")
		Loop
	BackToNormal:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN,0)	
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(FRIGHTENED,0)			
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("CultistIsCrawling",1)		
	See: 
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("CultistTaunt_Enemy",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("CultistIsCrawling",1,"Crawling")		
	SeeLoop:		
		YCUG A 1 A_Chase("", "Missile",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE) 
		YCUG A 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUG A 1 A_Chase 
		YCUG A 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUG B 1 A_Chase 
		YCUG B 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUG B 1 A_Chase("", "Missile",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE) 
		YCUG B 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUG C 1 A_Chase 
		YCUG C 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUG C 1 A_Chase 
		YCUG C 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUG D 1 A_Chase("", "Missile",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE) 
		YCUG D 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUG D 1 A_Chase 
		YCUG D 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUG E 1 A_Chase 
		YCUG E 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUG E 1 A_Chase("", "Missile",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE) 
		YCUG E 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)

		YCUG F 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		YCUG F 1 A_Chase 
		YCUG F 1 A_Chase("", "",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		Loop
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(220,"FFF")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(450,"TNTT")

			YCUG G 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			YCUG G 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			Stop
	}
}

		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)

		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid

Actor Zealot : Cultist 
{
	Health 50
	PainChance 128
	+DONTRIP	
	DropItem "RandomZealotDrop"
	Obituary "%o was shocked by a Zealot."
	States 
	{ 
	Spawn:
		YCU0 A 0
		YCU0 A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
		YCU0 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
		YCU0 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
	Spawn2:	  
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,3)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(184,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("CultistIsCrawling",1)
		TNT1 AA 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("CultistTaunt_Enemy",1,"Curse")		
	SpawnLoop:	
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("CultistIsCrawling",1,"SpawnCrawl")	
		YCU0 A 5 A_Look
		Loop	
	SpawnCrawl:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(FRIGHTENED,0)	
	SpawnCrawlLoop:
		YCU1 N 5 A_Look 
		Loop		
	Curse:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("CultistGotYou",CHAN_VOICE,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("CultistTaunt_Enemy",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("CultistIsCrawling",1)			
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(FRIGHTENED,0)		
	RoamLoop:	
		YCUJ A 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look
		YCUJ A 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ A 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ A 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ B 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ B 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ B 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ B 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ C 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ C 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ C 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ C 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ D 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ D 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ D 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look
		YCUJ D 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ E 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ E 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ E 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ E 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ F 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ F 1 A_Wander
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
		YCUJ F 1 A_Wander 
		TNT1 A 0 A_Look

Actor ZealotTesla : TeslaProjectile 
{
	Speed 35
	Scale 0.50
	DamageType ""
 	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_LoopActiveSound
			Goto SpawnLoop			
		SpawnLoop:	
			TESP AAAAAA 1 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("TeslaProjectileBall0",0,0,0,0,0,0,0)
			TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_FadeIn(0.16)
			TESP AAAAAA 1 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("TeslaProjectileBall0",0,0,0,0,0,0,0)
			TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_FadeIn(0.16)			
			TESP AAAAAA 1 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("TeslaProjectileBall0",0,0,0,0,0,0,0)			
			Loop
		Death:
			TNT1 AAAAA 1 A_SpawnItemEx("TeslaFX_Zealot", random(-8,8), random(-8,8), random(0,3), random(-12,12), random(-12,12), random(0,3))
			Stop
	}
}

		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodPriest_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodPriest_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodPriest_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodPriest_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodPriest_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("VULNERABLE", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("SHOOTABLE", 0)
		Goto ShrunkLoop
	ShrunkLoop:
		TNT1 A 2 A_JumpIfInventory("MasterDeadToken",1,"ShrunkDie")
		loop
	ShrunkDie:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 1 A_Die("Shrink")
		stop
	Death.Shrink:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 1 A_KillMaster
		stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		YCU7 A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoop
	ExpanderLoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		loop
	ExpanderPop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		YCU7 A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}
}
